# ShrimpDev Architecture Map

_Generated by R3239 on 20260110_214711_

## Persistence (INI)
- `docs/ARCHITECTURE_PERSISTENCE.md`


## Canonical runtime registry

- `registry/ShrimpDev.ini` (canonical INI)

- `registry/ShrimpDev.ini.bak` (backup)


## High-level layout

- `main_gui.py`: main entry point / UI

- `modules/`: application modules (logic, docking, persistence, runners)

- `tools/`: runner scripts (R####.cmd + R####.py)

- `Reports/`: runner & diagnostics reports

- `registry/`: runtime state (INI etc.)

- `docs/`: documentation (this file)

<!-- R3540 BEGIN: Runner Relevance & Purge Policy -->
## Runner Relevance & Purge Policy (Housekeeping)

**Entry-Flow (vereinfachtes Modell):**
- UI (Toolbar) → `modules/toolbar_runner_exec.py` → Runner-Aufruf
- UI-Events starten Runner **nicht** direkt via `subprocess/os.system`

**Relevance Sources (verbindlich):**
- ✅ `modules/` = operative Relevanz (Entry-Graph/Executor/Core)
- ✅ `registry/` = explizite Relevanz (Allowlist/Registry)
- ❌ `tools/` = **keine** Relevanzquelle (Runner-Querverweise sind nicht runtime)

**Purge Flow (High-Level):**
1) Scan (modules/ + registry/ + config) → runtime-referenced IDs
2) Add protections (last-N, allowlist)
3) Move candidates → Archiv (no delete)
4) Report: moved/kept/missing (reproduzierbar)

**Stabilität/Guards:**
- Busy/Single-Run Schutz verhindert Parallelstarts (Double-Click, TK_CALLBACK Chaos).

<!-- R3540 END -->

<!-- R3566 BEGIN -->
### Purge entrypoint guard (UI)

`modules/ui_toolbar.py` performs a hard guard before starting Purge:
- verifies `registry/tools_keep.txt` exists (canonical)
- blocks Purge if missing
<!-- R3566 END -->
